Roman&quot;;">二、本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放的<span lang="EN-US">39</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">三、本期获悉狱中<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人的动态信息（附简历）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、黄雪琴、<a name="_Hlk169766260">王建兵</a>、许健、陈文胜<span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张春雷、涂金灿、季孝龙、李怀庆、王炳章、何方美、宋泽、徐琳<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">狱中动态信息通报：<span _Hlk159664181;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四、本期新增被刑事拘留、强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五、本期新增被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">23</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">七、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本期中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">1714</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引</span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日共收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3380</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">8</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">八年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">105</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千字</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">39</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留、强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">23</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">25</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1714</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk162569632"></a><a name="_Hlk162449568"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 11.0pt;">、本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放的<span lang="EN-US">39</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span><p _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张敏杰：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海公民，是一位建筑工程师，曾经负责上海最高建筑物金茂大厦现场施工工程监理。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张敏杰因在推特发表“和平转型建议”相关言论，被徐汇区政保人员约谈。随后，他将谈话内容发布推特。但第二天<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日中午，张敏杰在住家附近公园锻练身体时被抓捕，随即被抄家。当日，张敏杰被上海市公安局徐汇分局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，被羁押在上海市徐汇区看守所。后其于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/20245.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/20245.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白玉珍：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省信阳市浉河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在看守所遭开庭。靳玉玲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁；白玉珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。白玉珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡玉嫦：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，家住汕头市龙湖区外砂镇莲中村。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，原本幸福温馨的家，被中共迫害得支离破碎。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被金平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元；蔡玉嫦提起上诉；汕头市中级法院<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日枉法维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日左右，蔡玉嫦被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450658.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，唐山市农机局退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在中共当局的“敲门行动”中，他被唐山市路北区文化路派出所警察绑架。警察非法抄家持续了三个小时，家中大量私人物品被抢劫。在警察绑架过程中，曹进兴被摔伤，缝了几针。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕，在唐山市第一看守所被关押一年多，后背生了很多皮疹。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，河北唐山市路北区一审判处曹进兴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李立壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李立壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李立壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：丁燕被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，范学斌刑满出狱仅一年五个月，就又遭警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年其又遭抓捕，随即又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。在狱中其遭酷刑虐待，以至于现在双腿也不能站立行走。范学斌现被关押在辽宁省大连监狱。据悉，范学斌已被监狱迫害致不能行走，须用轮椅代步。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，江西赣州法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">720</span>中共迫害法轮功以来，她不放弃大法修炼，去北京上访，坚持向世人、向政府官员讲法轮功，发送大法真相资料和《九评》等，先后<span lang="EN-US">12</span>次被抓、被关押或被诬判，其中<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被劳教（累计<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年），也多次被抓捕在赣州看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，章贡区公安局国保大队抓捕在家的顾秀芳，并抄了她的家，没有出示任何证件。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年初被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442548.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442548.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李立壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李立壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李立壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：焦其华被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，金丽燕与肖传雄、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月其被取保候审，后因其继续从事法轮功宣传活动，又被收监逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，金丽燕被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林立盛：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省茂名市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次抓捕林立盛。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉茂南区公检法合谋对林立盛判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/3/454462.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省鹤岗市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日刘玉秋在家被当地警察断电抓捕，关押在鹤岗市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月得知刘玉秋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，已被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">17/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk170454977"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑丹增</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">（藏<span lang="EN-US">/</span>左贡寺高僧）：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年左右出生，西藏自治区昌都市左贡县旺达镇乌雅村人，又称乌雅•朱古（即转世喇嘛）洛桑丹增仁波切，早年曾在阿里地区任职导游和司机，后成为西藏左贡寺高僧。曾因经常到西藏的左贡县左贡寺劝导僧俗民众停止供奉所谓的“朵杰凶天”，而要为西藏民族的长远理想和第十四世达赖喇嘛的健康长寿着想，并鼓励藏人努力保护、发扬民族宗教与文化等，受到藏人僧俗的广泛爱戴和尊敬，随招致中共当局的恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在西藏拉萨市被左贡县警方抓走刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，被西藏自治区左贡县法院以“追随达赖分裂集团”、“劝诫、蛊惑地方藏民停止修供凶天”等为罪由，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk52322614"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">18/</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322614;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗建荣：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322614;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西省南城县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生。江西省南城县洪门镇付前村人。罗建荣从<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始修炼至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，在修炼不到十年的时间，曾经被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">19/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk170455106"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东珠海市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，女，江西省抚州市人，家住广东珠海市香洲区情侣北路。马丽娜是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，她在珠海市香洲区山峰路附近发放法轮功法轮功资料时，遭社区人员恶告。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，她在家中被香洲区公安分局国保抓捕，并被抄家<span lang="EN-US">.</span>。随后马丽娜被关押到香洲区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，她被香洲区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，马丽娜被香洲区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，被罚金三千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/11/454762.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川绵阳市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，四川绵阳市北川县人，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共邪党开始迫害法轮功后，他多次被抓捕、关押，曾两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，母志太被绵阳市涪城区公安警察抓捕。涪城区公安警察抄了他儿子的房屋和他自己的租房屋，抢走很多私人财产。母志太被关押在绵阳市看守所近半年。绵阳市涪城区法院在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日对母志太庭审。律师在法庭上为母志太做了无罪辩护。未当庭宣判。后得知其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span><a class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，马楼派出所警察闯到司太安家实施抓捕，将独自一人在家的司太安押到鲁山县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，司太安在鲁山县看守所内被鲁山县法院庭审，法官不让家人参加，不许律师做无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁。辽宁朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，朝阳市公安局，政法委，<span lang="EN-US">610</span>秘密开会策划迫害，预谋在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。王忠学、吴艳玲夫妇是其中两个，吴艳玲被关押在朝阳市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被凌源市法院远程视频开庭。后得知：吴艳玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: Roman&quot;;">项本子：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">工作在广东深圳，原籍湖北省麻城市的法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，曾经两次在福建省被分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半和<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午，在广东省深圳市住宿处，被广东省东莞市长安区乌沙派出所警察，联合广东省国保和东莞市国保，抓捕。项本子被关押在东莞市第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>看守所。据说是因两个月前，项本子在东莞市长安区发放大法法轮功资料，被监控和跟踪。后遭东莞市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，项本子被关押到广东省韶关市北江监狱迫害。之后，家人多次向北江监狱提出会见，监狱方以项本子是法轮功学员，是严管期，不可会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">29/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秀娟：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">法轮功学员徐秀娟，家在秦皇岛市北港镇，女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十来岁，因为信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被中共警察抓捕，关押在秦皇岛市第一看守所。被抓捕后，现在在公安医院监护中，徐秀娟的身体处于危险状态，高血压、贫血、心衰，血压最高达到二百四十。亲朋好友一直在找看守所和法院交涉。但是他们互相推诿，拿法轮功学员的生命当儿戏。徐秀娟于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被庭审，遭海港区法院、秦皇岛中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被关押到河北石家庄女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，河南方城县公安局伙抓捕了许朝晖，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许朝晖</span>被关押<span Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">35/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张清香：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">36/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张树德：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">37/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在甘肃女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张雪莲，被国保警察抓捕到敦煌看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，敦煌法院去看守所，宣读对张雪莲的判决结果：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom:
