style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陈文胜、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>王建兵：女权活动家黄雪琴、劳工行动者王建兵被以“煽动颠覆国家政权”罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，本网获悉：女权活动家<a name="_Hlk169766216">黄雪琴和劳工行动者王建兵</a>“煽动颠覆国家政权”案今天上午在广州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，一审判决黄雪琴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王建兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。黄雪琴当庭表示要上诉。其判决书一审判决如下：一、被告人黄雪琴犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处沒收个人财产人民币十万元。刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止<span lang="EN-US">; </span>二、被告人王建兵犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利年，并处沒收个人财产人民币五万元刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/536.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/536.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1988</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年生，女权人士、独立记者，曾任《新快报》及《南都周刊》的调查记者，关注性别、平权、官员贪污、企业污染、弱势群体等议题，也参与多起<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>案件的报道和为性侵害性骚扰受害人提供帮助和支持。黄雪琴本计划于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年赴香港大学就读法学硕士，但后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被广州警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后改指定居所监视居住至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，黄成功获得英国志奋领奖学金支持，原计划于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往萨塞克斯大学（<span lang="EN-US">Universityof Sussex</span>）就读发展学硕士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日黄雪琴遭广州警方抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭审理，未当庭宣判。黄雪琴、王建兵“煽动颠覆国家政权”案<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午在广州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，一审判决黄雪琴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王建兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。黄雪琴当庭表示要上诉。一审判决书如下：被告人黄雪琴犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处沒收个人财产人民币十万元。刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建兵简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1983</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年生，甘肃天水人，独立公益人、劳工行动者。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业后，便加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯。曾担任西部阳光基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，作为青少年成长项目和残障社群赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关社区项目工作。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年起开始关注职业病工人的权益倡导和服务性工作，提供必要的法律支持。王也是国内<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日王建兵、黄雪琴遭广州警方抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭审理，未当庭宣判。黄雪琴、王建兵“煽动颠覆国家政权”案<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午在广州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，一审判决黄雪琴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王建兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。黄雪琴当庭表示要上诉。一审判决书如下：被告人王建兵犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利年，并处沒收个人财产人民币五万元刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许健：江苏省南通市维权人士许健获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，本网获悉：江苏省南通市维权人士许健日前被江苏南通市海门法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，海门许健被控寻衅滋事案在海门法院开庭。近日，有消息传出许健被海门区法院判处有期徒刑两年有余</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/2_27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/2_27.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许健简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">江苏省南通市维权人士。其妻子江苏省南通市海门区海门街道海兴新村<span lang="EN-US">207</span>幢<span lang="EN-US">501</span>室的朱培娟，因<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日海门区复兴新村一起管道液化气爆炸事件中，导致一直由她赡养照顾的叔叔朱中云烧伤死亡，公安机关没有公正处理而开始维权。该起管道液化气爆炸事件，不仅造成了朱培娟叔叔死亡，及另外两人一人重伤一人轻伤的后果，朱云中的遗体至今还在殡仪馆。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">16</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分左右，朱培娟在河北省廊坊市的出租房睡觉，被南通海门公安局截访人员以“网上通缉犯”之名，骗取辖区廊坊文安县滩里派出所民警撬开房间锁，强行将正在休息的朱培娟绑架回南通海门的，然后以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”指定监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初许健为此替妻子聘请律师到检察院申请立案监督，被海门区公安局治安拘留八天，结果<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日到期当局没有放许健回家，后家中老人收到刑事拘留通知书，称许健涉嫌寻衅滋事犯罪。许健在被羁押近半年后，其被控寻衅滋事案在海门区法院开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk169787161"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈文胜</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南衡阳基督徒陈文胜被控组织、资助非法聚集罪案今宣判 陈文胜获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，本网获悉：湖南衡阳基督徒陈文胜于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月遭刑事拘留，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被以涉嫌罪名是组织、资助非法聚集罪执行逮捕。后遭起诉、开庭，在今天<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午宣判了，陈文胜弟兄被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。陈文胜弟兄表示要上诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/17_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/17_20.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈文胜简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1969</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省衡阳市石鼓区人，住衡阳市石鼓区西湖一村，基督徒，湖南衡阳小群教会信徒，街头传道人，中国在押良心犯。早年曾吸毒成性十余年，后因在戒毒所听到福音而成为基督徒，并凭信心而除掉了毒瘾，故而自此致力于广传基督教福音；曾因经常举着写有“荣耀救主”、“悔改信靠得救”的十字架独自上街宣传，或与教会其他基督徒一起走街串巷，到城市闹市区（甚至到过西藏）传福音，随屡遭当局打压，多次被警方警告、威胁和被关押在衡阳市拘留所，甚至一年之中竟有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因到广西壮族自治区宣传基督教福音，而被南宁市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因上街传福音，而被湖南省衡阳市石鼓区警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，因与另一基督教信徒一起先后在衡阳市商业步行街附近和中医医院附近，利用喇叭、广播播放及发福音单张等方式宣传基督教，而被衡阳市蒸湘区警方以“扰乱社会秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因与其母为跨农历新年传福音，而被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；之后，因其继续走街串巷传福音，而在该年又曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因到浙江省传福音，而被辖区警方跨境抓捕，后被指定居所监视居住于西湖山庄，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天后，才在轮番轰炸般的约谈之后予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其到云南向少数民族朋友传福音，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，即被云南省文山壮族苗族自治州文山市警方拦截，且被移交给衡阳市警方遣回原籍；获释后，其接续外出传福音，甚至向国保警方和当地街道办事处工作人员等传福音；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其到湖南省益阳市安化县传福音，被衡阳市政法委、统战部及国保警方联合跨区抓回，次日被衡阳市青山派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其重获自由，但释放当天又去上街传福音；据悉，其妻子、儿媳及孙女等家人因受牵连，曾遭当局多次恐吓和威胁，被要求务必说服、阻止其外出传福音，否则不仅儿媳会被单位开除公职，而且其孙女也会在将来不能考取国家公务员与教师等工作；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因在街头传福音被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，期满后旋即又被以涉嫌“组织、资助非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被正式批捕。后遭起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。现羁押于衡阳市衡东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><a name="_Hlk170538828"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></a></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷、涂金灿、季孝龙、李怀庆、王炳章、何方美、宋泽、徐琳<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷：紧急关注：羁押已超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、至今未判的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老看守所患肝硬化<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日本网获悉：羁押已超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、至今未判的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老看守所患肝硬化。杨爱清师母通报如下：近日，贵阳市中级人民法院终于通知张春雷长老的辩护律师在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日前往阅卷。法院提供了之前开庭出示的案卷材料和庭审笔录，但表示之前庭审没有录音。法官因故外出。法官助理等工作人员态度较好，律师阅卷一整天未受干扰。据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭时，没有任何一个“证人”或者“被害人”获得出庭机会。张春雷长老为张展姊妹出狱感恩。他的身体状况不容乐观。在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年底，因胆囊炎等疾病住院一个多月，输液<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天，当时就查出了肝硬化。目前血压偏高。据悉，肝硬化是非常容易引发并发症的疾病，甚至危及存活年限。家属和律师紧急向法官反映了该情况。杨爱清师母表示张春雷长老以前没有肝胆类的患病记录。他鼓励贵阳的弟兄姊妹要喜乐，不要以他坐监为耻，要晓得一间教会长老可以为主坐监是很大的荣耀。请弟兄姊妹为他的身体和案件代祷，让他能早日出来就医，也让整个案件不至于错上加错。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/3_8.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/3_8.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生<span lang="EN-US">, </span>贵州省人，基督徒，贵阳市仁爱归正家庭教会主要组建人，教会带领人、长老，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》首批签名人之一，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因笃信耶稣基督，为广传基督教福音而与人共同组建了不从中共“三自教会”的“仁爱归正教会”；起初，该教会仅有几十会众，但在其不懈努力和事工（即神职人员在教会里所做的服务）带领下，因能热情广泛接待南来北往的信徒，故而在后来的国度事工中起到和发挥了重要的作用；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因积极参与由四川成都王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》的首批联署签名，随遭贵阳当局的严管监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其教会被贵阳市南明区民族宗教事务局突然取缔，并被指称，因其等一行人“未经批准，擅自以‘仁爱归正教会’名义在南明区中天商务港设立宗教场所，组织、举行宗教活动，接受宗教性捐献，违反《宗教事务条例》相关规定，责令停止宗教活动，拆除相关设施和标识”，最终致使其及教会信徒在失去会堂后只能在餐厅、酒店进行主日敬拜；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在当地某酒店举行主日聚会，而被数十名宗教局人员及警方先后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次连手冲击，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被封门，敬拜所用的十字架被强摘，其计算机等用品被查收；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因其教会新租房屋的房东再次被当局威胁，故而其被逼无奈只得再次从新租的房屋搬走；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其教会有十数名信众在参加小组学习时被突然闯入的贵阳市南明区民宗局人员和警方带走，遂其赶到派出所与警方交涉要人，不料竟遭粗暴野蛮对待，并被以“非法经营社团”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天；拘留期满时，又被贵阳市云岩区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被贵阳市云岩区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其妻子、儿子受牵连曾遭警方长时讯问且其妻遭虐待，教会多位同工成员亦遭抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其代理律师数次要求会见均受阻，被告知其“因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初遭起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭，未宣判。目前被羁押于贵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">涂金灿：北京资深民间出版人涂金灿被控涉嫌“非法经营罪”案已移送检察院<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，本网近日获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底被以”非法经营罪“刑事拘留的北京民间出版人涂金灿，经过北京海淀区公安局两次延长侦查期限，其案卷已于近日移送北京海淀区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_6.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_6.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">涂金灿简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京出版人。涂金灿<span lang="EN-US">,1962</span>年出生于湖北省孝感市，曾做过教师，后进行文化创业。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">,</span>涂金灿在北京创办“家谱传记机构”<span lang="EN-US">,</span>从事民间家谱、家史、传记的出书业务<span lang="EN-US">,</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被捕的<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年间<span lang="EN-US">,</span>已经为<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>多个普通百姓家庭整理出版了家谱、家史、个人传记类图书。他的事迹曾被新华社、《中国青年报》、《中国日报海外版》等官方媒体做过专题报道。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">,</span>时任总理李克强到海淀区创业大街视察<span lang="EN-US">,</span>还曾参观过涂金灿的“北京家谱传记文化馆”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年的三年疫情封控期间，涂金灿的民间出版业务遭到重大打击，仅靠借债勉强维持运作。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年疫情封控解除后，本以为业务能得到一些恢复，但当局的文化管制和经济勒索接踵而来。在被捕前，涂金灿已多次被海淀区文化部门、公安部门约谈，被海淀区公安局及中关村派出所查封图书仓库，公司承接的一部《何氏家谱》图书在邮寄发货后被海关查扣，以此为由进行罚款，但经过三年疫情，涂金灿及其公司已经债务累累，公司日常运作已经非常困难，根本没钱交纳罚款。当局的经济勒索没达到目的，就悍然动用司法手段，以刑事罪名抓捕了涂金灿，查封了“北京家谱传记机构”，导致公司停业员工失业。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被批捕。涂金灿先生十多年来一直在海淀区从事个人出书、老年修史的事业。曾出版过《何家栋纪念文集》、周舵论民主等书，他曾在<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年写作《中国何处去》被关押一年，是零八宪章第六批签署者。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者季孝龙案转监至上海市新收犯监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，本网获悉：季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日因替封城时的上海人民发声而遭抓捕，一审被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。季孝龙不服判决依法上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，上海第一中院就著名人权捍卫者季孝龙案作出二审判决——维持一审<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的判刑结果。随后季孝龙案转监至上海市新收犯监狱。目前，季孝龙已被转至判刑人员“集训”地——上海市新收犯监狱（具体地址：上海青浦区外青松路<span lang="EN-US">7935</span>号，电话<span lang="EN-US">021</span>一<span lang="EN-US">69207230</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">201701</span>）进行所谓“集训”。“集训”后会再分往其它监狱服刑。季孝龙上次获刑也是先被关进这里然后转至白茅岭监狱服刑，并在服刑期间受到长时间单独关押、不准消费等酷刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46_9.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46_9.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，维权公民，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑；据悉，羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体健康虚弱且生病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍亦遭拒收；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刑满获释；同年上海封城，其为上海市民持续发声。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，又被浦东新检察院以同罪名正式批捕，后季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被起诉。后已经开庭，未宣判。最终于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被一些寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，此前被羁押于浦东新区看守所，现转监至上海市新收犯监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆：获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的重庆民营企业家李怀庆又被转监到贵州省兴义监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的重庆民营企业家李怀庆又被转监到贵州省兴义监狱，此前李怀庆先生在贵州省六盘水市六盘水监狱服刑。家属未被告知，去六盘水监狱探监扑空。李怀庆妻子包艳今天通报：“<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日一大早和孩子去六盘水监狱看望先生，到监狱告知怀庆又被转到兴义监狱去了！作为家属的我们什么都不知道？到底为何这么频繁的转监狱！已经被重判了，还在怕什么！我们不得不连夜坐车去到兴义监狱！通信地址：贵州省兴义市<span lang="EN-US">00934</span>信箱附九号二监区二分监李怀庆收邮<span lang="EN-US">562400</span>，望朋友们相互告知，感谢。”重庆民营企业家、亿万富翁李怀庆，因在微信上说几句话，就被当局以煽动颠覆国家政权，及诈骗、敲诈勒索、非法拘禁等四项罪名羁押。在被关押近三年之后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在重庆市第一中级法院宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，令世人震惊。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/20.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1966</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，重庆市人，复转军人，“随手公益”的志愿者，重庆富华典当公司老板，民营企业家，中国在押政治犯。因个性急公好义，曾长期关注和资助弱势群体；曾因默默多年资助大凉山地区贫困儿童及家境困难的昔日战友，积极参与“大爱清尘”活动救助尘肺病工友，并为此先后捐资近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万元，不计回报，而深受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被重庆市警方突然以“涉黑” 罪名刑拘，其妻儿及公司职员等亦受牵连被抓，在被莫名其妙数时小时审讯、恐吓、威逼之后才得释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其名下公司、妻子包艳及与此案完全无关的其胞姊资产、账户（包括现金及房产等，总值上亿元）均被重庆警方以“打黑”名义冻结；后其罪名被重庆市检察院更换为涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”，指控其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾七度在微信“以造谣、诽谤等方式煽动颠覆国家政权”，包括转发“红四方面军在四川杀人百万”文章，又转发过有“道义抗争”、“暴力革命”等字眼的录音，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其罪名遂于“涉黑罪”变成“颠覆国家政权罪”；在其长达近两年的羁押过程中，其律师及其家属均未收到过任何有关其涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”的逮捕通知书或文件说明；后李怀庆涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在重庆市第一中级法院开庭审理，未宣判。目前李怀庆被羁押于重庆江北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日重庆民营企业家李怀庆被庆市第一中级法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法拘禁罪四项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。后被关押在贵州省六盘水市六盘水监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被转监到贵州省兴义监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王炳章：著名民运领袖、政治犯王炳章狱中情况通报：王炳章还活着但身体状况不佳<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，本网获悉已经入狱<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的著名民运领袖、政治犯王炳章狱中情况，现在通报如下：王炳章的弟弟今日通报了王炳章的狱中境况：王炳章还活着，但身体状况不佳。今天<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，是我的哥哥炳章被绑架坐牢<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的日子。妹妹最近在韶关监狱探望了哥哥，他身体虚弱、行走缓慢。自去年患上高血压后，高压时常达到<span lang="EN-US">200</span>，曾一度跌倒。家属异常担心他再次中风倒地不起。我们已经告知炳章：如果上述情况发生，我们全体家属会按照他的嘱咐：与律师、法医及全体家属前往中国验尸，追究中国政府的责任。我们全体家属永远与炳章同在，救助炳章永不放弃！直至他平安回到家中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_28.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_28.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王炳章简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1947</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河北省石家庄市籍人，基督徒，美国永久居民，民主异见人士，中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年曾在美国创办《中国之春》杂志，被捕前任中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被不明身份的人在越南绑架后带到中国境内被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被以“间谍和组织领导恐怖组织罪”被判无期徒刑；据悉，其在狱中长期被单独关押，身体受到极大迫害，期间大中风一次，小中风两次，并患上严重的过敏症，病发时气喘，过敏性鼻炎，喷嚏咳嗽打个不停，使肺部、胸腔受到很大伤害，常感生不如死，冬天则是长冻疮，唇疮，薄薄一堵墙，难御严寒；其多次要求换监均不允许，其家属数年要求探监，也被拒绝，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其弟王炳武才被准予代表家属与其会面<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分种，并得知其一直被单独关押在狱中小号里，既不知外界任何信息，也不能有任何书信往来；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其身体可能随出现生命危险，狱方已在其囚室安放了警报器，称其一旦感到有不适即马上警报；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，加拿大感恩节期间，其已在加拿大生活的胞弟终于收到中国大陆狱方获准会见通知书，称此应表明其兄还活着。目前在广东省韶关市北江监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美：代理律师会见狱中人权捍卫者何方美的情况通报：何方美非常担心孩子们的情况，希望自己能早点出去照顾孩子律师指出目前羁押程序是严重违法 极不人道 准备控告<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，律师会见了狱中人权捍卫者何方美，她表示辉县市法院王法官多次让她认罪认罚。何方美非常担心孩子们的情况，认为孩子们现在需要家庭的照顾，希望自己能早点出去照顾孩子。当日下午，律师到辉县市法院找王法官交涉，质问何方美自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月一审开庭至今，长达<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月里，为何没有收到任何延期审理等，目前的羁押程序是严重违法的。王法官未回应。律师指出：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月将何方美当庭逮捕就是违法的，因为她是几个未成年人的唯一抚养人，这种逮捕既违法，也是极不人道的！本案应该尽快处理。王法官说具体量刑要找检察院沟通，律师表示审理案件是法院应尽的职责，要对法院和法官违法进行控告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_49.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_49.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，河南省新乡市辉县人，网名“十三妹”，“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人，人权捍卫者。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其年仅<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月龄的小女打了百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助投诉均被拒，遂逐级维权讨说法，后因多地亦发生类似疫苗伤害宝宝事件，随组建“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体共同呼吁，以求当局关注并给予合理赔偿救治；然当局却对此一拖再拖，其被迫到北京上访，故屡遭抓捕打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，因中共两会期间与各地问题疫苗家长到北京王府井为残儿募捐，随被新乡市辉县警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被以辉县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转刑拘，关押在河南省新乡看守所；因期间一直拒绝认罪，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新乡市辉县检察院以同罪名批捕，后被起诉并罗列<span lang="EN-US">6</span>项罪，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在河南省辉县法院正式开庭；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被辉县检察院以“事实不清、证据不足”为由撤诉，后被无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因其不断发声请求国家立法解决疫苗问题、呼吁联合国关注中国疫苗问题等，而在北京再度遭遇强迫失踪。后获释。同年，因当地政府阻挠其带疫苗致残的女儿出去看病，何方美于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日对辉县政府招牌泼墨抗议，被拘留。获释后，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日再次对辉县政府泼漆抗议。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，有消息称她被当地公安局软禁，但地址不详。此后不久，她的孩子和丈夫李新也被维稳人员带走，失去消息。一年多来，当局没有公布任何有关他们情况的信息。在何方美被拘留的时候，她已经怀孕七个月。一直处于遭强迫失踪状态。狱中产子，亦遭起诉开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月一审开庭至今，长达<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月未宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋泽：代理律师：宋泽案庭审情况通报<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2024</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>号宋泽案的庭审情况：早上<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点半左右我们两位律师陪同宋妈妈和他二姐一起来到区法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号审判庭，面积很小，两排座位大约可以坐<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人左右，宋妈妈和二姐被安排在后排靠墙的两个位置上，随即一法警紧挨着坐在一旁，整个法院似乎都在为这次开庭忙碌，法院大门外到处是法警，交警，片警和便衣。开庭前<span lang="EN-US">5</span>分钟我走出法院大门抽烟，身后也跟随三名法警，如此兴师动众戒备森严，不知他们意欲何为。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点正式开庭，宋泽被两名法警押送进法庭，宋妈妈就已经泣不成声，宋泽多次欲回头看母亲被法警制止。整个庭审中宋保持沉默，拒绝回答所有问题，但一直盯着他右前方的法庭监控显示屏，审判长多次提醒他要面对审判席，宋置之不理。后来我才发现，那个显示屏上有他妈妈的影像。本人发表了无罪辩护意见并就关键问题与公诉人开展了两轮辩论。庭审结束后，长沙市司法局一黄姓工作人员突然出现在审判庭，并邀请我们两位辩护人去<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号法庭隔壁的审判庭谈话，我才知道，武汉方面政法系统的相关人员一直在这个法庭通过视频观看庭审直播，长沙市司法局派员赶赴武汉也在一同观看。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_22.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋泽简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名宋光强，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，湖北襄阳人，自称襄阳宋泽。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>毕业于中南财经政法大学，法学、经济学双学士。公盟负责人、新公民运动的参与者、倡导者。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年大学毕业后，宋泽曾在一家德资电梯企业武汉的办事处做商务行政事务工作，后又在深圳一家私营评估企业总经理办公室从事助理。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宋泽向许志永写信，申请加入公盟，随后以志愿者的身份工作。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年冬宋泽一直在从事救助访民的工作，给访民捐助物资补给援助，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年开始了披露和救助被北京黑监狱关押的访民，维权人士。并在两会前期编绘了北京黑监狱地图。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽因给访民送汤圆而被警方带走，后不久被放出。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，宋泽与赵振甲等十多人冲进湖南郴州驻京办的「黑监狱」，解救出被非法关押的<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的龚江保、<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁的于洪和<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁的陈碧香等三位上访人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点宋泽在北京南站等候一位求助者的约见时，被北京公安数位警察强制带走，据宋泽本人描述应该是北京市公安局有预谋的计划。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，北京市公安局以「寻衅滋事罪」将宋泽刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天，羁押在丰台区看守所。但是期限满时，公安局没有放人，而是将刑拘转为「监视居住」，期限六个月，至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到期。许志永认为宋泽被捕是因为救助被关押在黑监狱的三位老人和陈光诚的侄子陈克贵的妻子。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日身为公盟志愿者的宋泽被失踪，后来刘卫国律师偶然发现宋泽被关押在北京市公安局第三拘留所，涉嫌「聚众扰乱社会秩序」罪。宋泽在狱中被赵姓副队长国保殴打，方式为扇耳光、拳打脚踢，无任何人制止。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽的律师李金星、张磊联名向北京市检察院、最高检察院、公安部等部门提出了就北京市公安局有关警员涉嫌故意伤害、徇私枉法、虐待被监管人犯罪的控告状。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日宋泽由其舅舅到北京为其担保取保候审，在被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月零<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天后，走出了北京市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日焦作访民张小玉、许有臣案发生，为了查明真相和声援弱势群体，宋泽等人发起了公民声援团，宋泽提供账户，为张小玉案进行募捐。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日北京警方对道衡律师事务所进行抄家，将余文生律师、王成律师、宋泽、李对龙律师四人抓走。王成律师、李对龙律师不久获释。余文生律师和宋泽遭刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日宋泽被以取保候审的名义获释，结束了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多月的羁押，宋泽在押期间一直保持零口供。宋泽于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被武汉市公安局以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，在宋泽被抓四个月后，律师在武汉市第二看守所会见了他，被羁押是因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和提供侵入非法计算机信息系统程序、工具罪。案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日已被武汉市武昌区检察院提起起诉。宋泽案将于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在武汉开庭审理。宋泽现羁押于武汉市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳：广州民主人士、词曲作家、人权捍卫者徐琳先生已被正式批捕<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，本网获悉：广州民主人士、词曲作家、人权捍卫者徐琳先生于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭广州市公安局南沙区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，一个月后其已经被正式批捕。现羁押在广州市南沙看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_32.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_32.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖南省株洲市人，诗人，哲学研究者，广东网络作家，独立中文笔会成员，民主异议人士，中国良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末即开始撰写时政文章，诗歌及创作歌曲，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年始又在广州，深圳等地积极开展街头举牌，演讲，组织公民集会等活动<span lang="EN-US">;</span>近年来，因与维权公民刘四仿合作，创作并出品了多个以自由，人权，法治为内容的歌曲，颇受自由民主爱好者喜爱与欢迎，遂引起广东当局强烈不满，并成为维稳严控的对象，曾遭多次非法拘禁和秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">;2012</span>年，曾因将浙江异见人士朱虞夫所作诗歌“是时候了”改编谱曲为“就是现在”，引起网友广泛关注和转载而被广州警方于同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪“刑拘，羁押于广州市番禹看守所，指控其罪行比广州上街举牌还要严重，具有明显煽动群众上街意向，情节十分严重<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日又被广东省当局改为秘密监视居住它处，期间其家属多次要求当局出示书面通知及关押地点，竟都遭拒<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾参与民主人士王登朝发起的<span lang="EN-US">'</span>莲花山公园千人公民集会<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，计划于活动现场发表政治演讲，不料事前却遭当局绑架，后被秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">;2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因发布“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”大抓捕事件而创作的歌曲“正义律师之歌”触怒当局，其任职公司因受当局施压而遭失业，并被绑架至广州软禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大召开前夕，其在湖南老家照顾患病父亲时突然被广州市南沙区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，其广州住所被查抄，搜走计算机，手机，书籍，笔记本等个人物品；次日，与其一起创作歌曲的搭档刘四方也被江西省宜春市警方以同理由抓走；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被广州市南沙区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，关押在广州市南沙区看守所；据悉，被押期间遭酷刑，从<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日每天都被警方三班倒提讯；一直零口供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被广州市南沙区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。此前其在广东省佛山市高明监狱服刑。徐琳先生又于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭广州市公安局南沙区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其已经被正式批捕。现羁押在广州市南沙看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留及强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙治军、刘少明、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、孙治军：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州维权人士。孙治军曾因公开举报孙庄村征地补偿款<span lang="EN-US">9600</span>百多万，被非法截留挪用，被郑州市中原区人民法院打击报复判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。孙治军出狱后继续维权上访，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午，在北京青季酒店，被河南郑州市中原区公安局民警暴力抬走绑架，视频显示一辆京<span lang="EN-US">Q6k8Z0</span>黑色轿车旁，有五六名未穿制服的彪形大汉，把孙治军强行塞到轿车里。目前遭绑架的孙治军音信全无。在中共二十届三中全会即将召开前夕，孙治军这次的被绑架失踪后命运令人担忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_83.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_83.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、刘少明：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名“木星上行”，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，安徽安庆市怀县人，因纪念八九六四及发表言论被行政拘留多次和判刑二年，出狱后一直被当局打压，被当地公安系统当作维稳升迁发财的敲门砖。因缺乏关注不为外界所关注，刘少明在六四<span lang="EN-US">35</span>周年前夕再度失踪至今。手机<span lang="EN-US">15391830716</span>已经停机，所有社交账号停止状态。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/35_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/35_25.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk167930243"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五、</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">23</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">姜春林、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刑期不明：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">付金凤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜春林：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">或名姜春林。山东省青岛市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，家住青岛市崂山区北村社区。姜春林<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午十点半左右，姜纯林驱车到儿子开的饭店帮忙。大约十一点左右，三名便衣警察闯入店内，在没出示任何手续的情况下强行将他带走。随后警察去姜春林家抄家，抄走一台打印机、电脑、大法书籍和一本“修炼心得”笔记本。第二天，警察以监控录像上有一背包男子背影像姜春林，推断他在社区散发真相资料，以此作为“证据”将他刑事拘留，把他关押到即墨普东看守所。姜春林的妻子因患脑血栓，已瘫痪在床六年，因受姜春林被捕的时警察抄家的惊吓，十天后便撒手人寰，终年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉，姜纯林已被中共青岛市公、检、法机构合谋判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并被劫转监到山东济南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/7.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘振刚：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">网名刘子德。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，河南汤阴人，因参与四川泸州秘密组党，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被抓捕。四川泸州地区<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月间发生大型抓捕事件，目前已知十余人随后均以“颠覆国家安全罪”被判刑，具体抓捕多少人尚无详细资料。刘振刚是<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月大抓捕中被捕的一员，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30 </span>日被四川省泸州市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行逮捕，关押在泸州市看守所。后刘振刚获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期应至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月左右。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/55.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"
