style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">路刚：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北邢台市巨鹿县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，家住巨鹿县阎疃镇寨里村。路刚是<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始修炼法轮功的。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，他因向百姓宣讲法轮功遭迫害的真相，被中共警察抓捕，被邢台市广宗县法院判刑五年、在河北省冀东监狱服刑，历经非人的酷刑折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年才刑满回家。路刚<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在家中被闫疃镇派出所警察与巨鹿县国保大队警察抓捕、关押在巨鹿县看守所。后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，家属被电话告知路刚已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，送往唐山冀东监狱。整个过程，家属没有收到任何法律手续。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_22.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜亮明：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1948</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁，忻州家庭教会牧师。杜牧师于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被刑事拘留，罪名为组织他人偷越国边境罪，后被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。目前在山西省阳泉监狱服刑。其妻子魏秀平师母今年<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁，牧师被捕后脑梗，精神明显受打击。几年来一直由教会弟兄姊妹白天黑夜轮流陪伴。师母近期去监狱探视，杜亮明牧师在里面挺好，让师母多运动，照顾好自己。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/576.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/576.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk168927256"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk168927256;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜永芹</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林市法轮功学员，女，出生于一九六九年十月，毕业于吉林大学机械系。她考入兰州大学攻读硕士研究生，毕业后在浙江理工大学任教。早年修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月二十日中共江泽民集团发动对法轮功的迫害以来，姜永芹多次遭到中共<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室、国家安全机关、国保、警察和街道居委会的骚扰，还被判刑三年，导致她的家庭和生活受到了巨大的伤害，长期无法工作。后来她定居在吉林省吉林市昌邑区。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，姜永芹女士被吉林市龙潭分局新安派出所警察抓捕，并关押在吉林市龙潭区水部宾馆的<span lang="EN-US">102</span>号房间。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日或<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，她被套上黑头套，并被带到秘密地点。吉林省公安厅的两名“特训室”警察与吉林市公安局国保大队的两名警察，最初采用了灌芥末和烟呛熏等酷刑手段对姜永芹进行酷刑折磨。之后，他们还采取下流手段对姜永芹进行性侵犯、猥亵和胁迫，持续折磨了近两个小时，给姜永芹造成了巨大的身心伤害。姜永芹的丈夫在海外奔走呼吁，要求无罪释放姜永芹，并严惩实施酷刑和猥亵罪行的相关公职人员。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，由多名维权律师组成的律师团对姜永芹遭受酷刑的吉林省公安厅和吉林市公安局公职人员提出控告，分别递交控告信至吉林市检察院、监察委员会、人大、政法委员会和妇女联合会，但多数部门拒绝接收或拖延处理。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，姜永芹遭吉林市昌邑区法院开庭，开庭没有通知家属，也不告知家属庭审结果。姜永芹的代理律师也被阻止出庭。姜永芹在关押期间遭到了严重的性迫害，她的辩护律师为此多方控告无果。由于姜永芹通过律师向海外媒体曝光了中共性侵害法轮功学员的特殊手段，当局禁止了姜永芹和外界的一切接触。至今快两年了，家人和律师都无法知道她的现状。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在没没有通知律师到场的情况下姜永芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_85.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_85.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">苏桂英：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东省湛江市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住湛江市麻章区湖光镇湖光农场。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，苏桂英开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，苏桂英因给民众发送法轮功真相资料，被湛江市赤坎区公安分局警察抓捕，后被湛江市赤坎区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。在广东省女子监狱被关押期间，她坚持信仰，不放弃修炼，遭残忍酷刑折磨：毒打、不让睡觉、踩脚趾头搓、牙签刺眼皮、冷水泼湿全身、掐捏、抓头撞铁门、手指甲掐捏肉体、抓住头发毒打、冻、饿、变态折磨、弹眼珠、刷全身包括阴部、洗衣粉刺激、开水烫、罚蹲（凳子倒插着铁钉）、药物迫害、关精神病院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年刑满出狱。苏桂英出狱后，发现自己当月的养老金就被湛江市麻章区社保局停发了。为了讨回公道，她一直维权上访。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，湛江市麻章区公安分局、志满派出所及麻章区政法委共<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人闯到苏桂英家将她抓捕。随后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。苏桂英于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭赤坎区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年重刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk169765651"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk169765651;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金新春</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖南省临澧县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁，原广播电视局退休职工。一九九七年六月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“七·二零”中共发动对法轮功的迫害后，金新春坚持修炼法轮功，先后七次遭抓捕关押，三次被判入狱，累计<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年半（<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月三年、<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月三年半、<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月五年）、被劳教一年半（<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月），在监狱、劳教所遭受心身折磨长达<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，被吊铐折磨的疤痕至今近二十年还清晰可见。金新春女士在牢狱中遭受折磨，九死一生，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出狱回家，可已经家破人亡：她丈夫和大儿子在长期痛苦的压力面前难以承受，先后在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月悲惨离世。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，临澧县公安局、安福镇派出所、望城乡派出所出动大量警力，到法轮功学员家进行抓捕，其中有金新春，随即被送到常德市看守所关押。后遭批捕、起诉，最终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬金新春被转监到湖南省长沙女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/5_20.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk168323356"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk168323356;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王慧琳</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">或名王会林，河北唐山法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁。唐山市丰南区黄各庄镇红花园村人，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年后，在中共迫害法轮功的二十多年中，王慧琳因坚持修炼，多次遭中共绑架，被劳教、判刑，在公安局、派出所、拘留所、看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受身心摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王慧琳被黄各庄派出所警察抓捕，后被送往唐山市丰南拘留所，她因身体原因，被拘留所拒收，后被放回家“监视居住”。后遭批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，卧炕不起的王慧琳竟然被滦南县法院人员来到家里开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。因身体原因一直未被收监。至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，王慧琳被黄各庄派出所警察再次抓捕，关押到唐山市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转监到河北省石家庄女子监狱，目前被关押在第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕庆：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁抚顺法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，吕庆原在抚顺石化系统工作，曾于二零一六年在家被抓捕，判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月，罚金一万元，被单位开除。吕庆<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在自己家楼下被东洲公安分局国保及东洲派出所警察抓捕、抄家，被关押在抚顺南沟看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，他被抚顺东洲法院在看守所开庭。吕庆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金一万八千元。吕庆正在上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46_12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/46_12.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张美菊：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">长春法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。一九九九年以前开始修炼法轮大法的，她在长春市绿园区环卫处工作。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日张美菊遭绿园区和平大街派出所警察入室抓捕。被关押在长春女子看守所。看守所不许家人见面。家人一直不知道张美菊的情况，看守所只是通知家人给被关押的张美菊存钱。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月得到消息，张美菊被长春市朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/4_12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈德光：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">甘肃省兰州市法轮功学员，男，一九四六年出生，原四冶西北分公司职工（已破产），家住兰州市红古区。他于一九九七年八月开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，陈德光曾多次被中共当局抓捕、关押，他被劳教、判刑，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受酷刑迫害，其中<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年七月他与妻子盛春梅一同被绑架构陷，夫妻俩被非法判刑九年。盛春梅在甘肃女子监狱被迫害致患严重的糖尿病、白内障、胆结石、化脓性胆囊炎，两耳失聪，双目失明，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日含冤离世；陈德光<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月才出冤狱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陈德光被兰州市公安局红古分局海石湾派出所警察入室抓捕，关押到海石湾看守所。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，兰州市红古区检察院给陈德光下发逮捕证，因陈德光进看守所就开始绝食抗议，生命垂危，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚上，他由家里人接回。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，陈德光被兰州市城关区法院庭审后遭收监；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被关押在海石湾看守所的陈德光再次被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月下旬获悉：陈德光已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年四月上旬被兰州市城关区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">夏明金</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">江西省南昌市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁，家住江西省南昌市青云谱区，一九九七年十二月开始修炼法轮功。因修炼法轮功，夏明金多次遭中共迫害，她曾被关押在洗脑班、拘留所，被劳教一年、遭判刑两年，还经常遭到“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”人员、青云谱区公安分局国保大队警察、岱山派出所片警、岱山司法所及施尧村社区等人员的骚扰。夏明金因外出给民众宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被南昌市公安局青云谱分局国保大队警察抓捕、抄家，之后她一直被关押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月下旬，家人得知夏明金已被南昌市西湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期，她已经被转监到江西省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/36.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b Roman&quot;;">13/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">祁开香：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖南省临澧县法轮功学员，女，一九四九年一月生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁，临澧县一完小退休教师，住临澧安福镇。一九九八年开始修法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“七·二零”中共发动对法轮功的迫害后，祁开香坚持修炼法轮功，多次遭迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年元月被警察关押到常德戒毒所强迫洗脑，县“六一零”又将她转到县拘留所，关押长达<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨她又被抓捕，关押在当地看守所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。她先后被县社保局停发、扣发社保养老金三年多。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出狱回家，每月只发给生活费<span lang="EN-US">962</span>元。她女儿受到恐吓导致<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年过早去世。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，临澧县公安局、安福镇派出所、望城乡派出所出动大量警力，到法轮功学员家进行抓捕，其中有祁开香。后遭批捕、起诉，最终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬祁开香被关押到湖南省长沙女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk170394141"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14/</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170394141;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">四川成都法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，一九八八年毕业于四川农业大学，他原在成都市新都区农村发展局农技中心工作，从一九九六年起，他开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，骆常勇被抓捕后，被龙泉驿区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，骆常勇在新都区斑竹园街道达利园食品厂附近被便衣抓捕。第二天被取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，新都检察院通知骆常勇去签字，据说是关于延长“取保候审”的时间，被骆常勇拒绝。由于不堪派出所和检察院的多次骚扰，骆常勇于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日离家出走。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，骆常勇在成都市成华区天回镇被抓捕。随即遭逮捕，关押在新都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，骆常勇被新都区法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并被罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/36_27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk168229487"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: Roman&quot;;">宋云玲</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">天津市法轮功学员，女，家住天津市河东区中山门街道团结北里。宋云玲因坚持法轮大法真善忍信仰，曾多次遭中共人员迫害，她约在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年期间，曾被关押在天津建新劳教所、板桥劳教所，期间她遭到暴力洗脑、关禁闭、不让睡觉等酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，宋云玲在订蛋糕时，要求店家在蛋糕上面写上“祝贺<span lang="EN-US">513</span>世界法轮大法日”的字样，结果遭人恶告。大直沽派出所警察在宋云玲取蛋糕时，对她进行录像、跟踪，继而在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日下午上门将她抓捕。关押在河东区看守所。在失去自由的两年里，她的丈夫、婆婆、姐夫相继因病离开人世。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被延寿县城北派出所警察抓捕到哈尔滨看守所关押，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前被关押在黑龙江女子监狱，据悉她被迫害得穿上尿不湿，情况待查。 刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，临澧县公安局、安福镇派出所、望城乡派出所出动大量警力，到法轮功学员家进行抓捕，其中有胡月英，随即被送到常德市看守所关押。后遭批捕、起诉，最终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬胡月英被转监到湖南省长沙女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李明华：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁省葫芦岛市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。原是葫芦岛市南票区大窝铺村的民办教师，执教有四、五年，自办幼儿园有十年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，她开始修炼法轮功。李明华老太太<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日乘车去看怀孕的女儿，安检时被抓捕、随后遭抄家，后被关押在葫芦岛看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日获悉：李明华于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被葫芦岛连山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，后李明华已被转监辽宁省第二女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/171.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/171.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">23/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">付金凤：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">江西南昌法轮功学员，女，原南昌市血站护师。<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，现年今年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，原南昌市血站护师，她于一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮大法。在中共邪党对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，她多次被抓捕、关押，曾两次遭劳教、两次遭判刑，在看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。付金凤女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日宣讲法轮功时遭人举报，被南昌市经开区蛟桥派出所警察抓捕。之后一直被关押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，付金凤已遭秘密判刑，刑期待查。目前付金凤已被转监到江西省女子监狱关押迫害。这是她第三次遭中共法院非法判刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span
